# Text Elements
a[i] = 2*a[j-k]


Assign(a[i], 2*a[j-k])

x = Assign(.  Access(a, i) , Op('*', 2, Access(a, Op('-', j, k) ) )  )

rvalue(x) = {
    z' = Node(t1); 
    emit string for Access(a, i) = z' 
    return z' <--
}

lvalue(Access(a, i)) = {
    return new Access(a, i); <--
}


rvalue(Op('*', 2, Access(a, Op('-', j, k)) ) = {
    t1;
    emit string for t1 = 2 * Node(t2); 
    return new Node(t1); <--
}

rvalue(Access(a, Op('-', j, k)) = {
    t2;
    new Access(j, Node(t3) ); gives Access(y, z') 
    emit string for t2 = Access( a, Node(t3)); 
    return new Node(t2); <--
}

lvalue(Access(a, Op('-', j, k)) = {
    return new Access(j, Node(t3) ); <--
}

rvalue(Op('-', j, k)) = {
    t3
    emit string t3 = j - k; 
    return new Node(t3) <--
}


"t3 = j - k;"
"t2 = Access( a, Node(t3));"
"t1 = 2 * Node(t2);"
"Access(a, i) = Node(t1);"



rvalue(x) = Node(t1);


"t3 = j - k;"
"t2 = a[t3];"
"t1 = 2 * t2;"
"a[i] = t1;"



























 ^pSQlGNdD

get(w): searching for w from B2(the curr environment))
loop through each env upward until Null or first w is found.
 ^8fAKXG3X

B0.prev = null
global environment ^MERE3w3s

B1.prev = B0 ^Hktl9QuX

B2.prev = B1 ^D5ANC0Zn

B4.prev = B0 ^0g7fxCWO

B3.prev = B0 ^NQDlqf9F

restore top to the saved env when we finish ^uILogMmF

new env when entering a new block ^9rurHYhW

saves the prev env to restore back when we finish this block ^B1t0G7Rf

left recursive productions 
for supporting any num of
 declarations/statements
 consecutively ^O2XzXUOP

note: these are the same production ^S2Td3PYD

new symbol that stores the type for the id ^DK7pNSxG

factor fetches the id from symbol table ^5aeR2XGz

program -> block, program is just 1 block in this book.
so the env outside the very first block(prev of the first block) is null;
top denotes the top of the chain of symbol tables. ^iFliyY0V
